With the introduction of objects in TradeStation 9= .0, the GlobalDictionary class was intro= duced that can be used to share information across applications (and betwee= n windows within the same application - for example, sharing data between 2= charts, 2 RadarScreen windows, etc.) within the TradeStation platform. If= you only need to share information within TradeStation (i.e., you don't ne= ed to share information between TradeStation and other programs outside of = TradeStation), it is recommended that the Globa= lDictionary be used since it is an engineered solution to data shari= ng within the TradeStation platform.



Here is the latest release of = GlobalVariable.dll - one of the D= LL coding demonstrations we provide for those who wish to create TradeStati= on-compatible DLL's. Important: The new functionality for the 6= 4-bit integer is available for TradeStation 9.0, Build 8816 and later. For= prior versions of TradeStation, use GlobalVariable 2.2. The 2.2 Version ca= n be found here:

https://community.t= radestation.com/discussions/Topic.aspx?Topic_ID=3D32115


T= he attached zip file contains the following:
  1. New document= ation (contained in the file "Global Variable 2.3.doc")


  2. A demonstration workspace (9.0, Build 8816 and= later)


  3. An ELD file containing studies and functions for = import


  4. C++ project and code files


  5. GlobalVariable.dll (compiled from the new Version 2.3 code)


ZIP FILE: Global Variable 23.ZIP



=
After clicking on the zip file link above, select "Save" (when p= rompted) in order to save the zip file to your local hard-drive. Use a util= ity such as WinZip=C2=AE to decompress the file.


Whe= n using Windows Vista or Windows 7, you may have to disable User Account Co= ntrol (UAC )(setting it to "never notify") for the DLL to be recognized. Ho= wever, you should exercise care in doing this and, if you do it at all, do = it only temporarily, as this is a security feature of Windows 7. Also, don'= t forget that, after changing UAC settings, the computer must be re-booted = for the new settings to take effect.

Also, note that if you are u= sing the 64-bit version of Windows 7, copy/paste the DLL in the following d= irectory (or equivalent):

C:\WINDOWS\SysWOW64\


Here= 's what's new in this version. Please see the documentation contained in t= he zip files for more detail:
  1. Increased the number of max= imum shared named global variables (MAXSHAREDNAMED ) from 3,000 to 10,000.
    2. =

  2. Added EasyLanguage functions to utilize the Int64 data type fo= r 64-bit integers:
    1. GVGetInteger64

    2. GVGet= Int64NameByNum

    3. GVGetNamedInt64

    4. GVGetNamedInt64ByN= um

    5. GVResetAllNmdInt64

    6. GVSetInteger64

      7. GVSetNamedInt64


  3. Added C++ functions to the DLL= to utilize the Int64 data type for 64-bit integers:
      GV_GetInteger64
    1. GV_GetInt64NameByNum

    2. GV_GetNamed= Int64

    3. GV_GetNamedInt64ByNum

    4. GV_ResetAllNmdInt64
    5. GV_SetInteger64

    6. GV_SetNamedInt64


Please refer to the extensive documentation file, "Global Variable 2.3.doc", which is included in the d= ownload package, for installation instructions and an introduction to how t= he global va= riable code works. If the documentation does not answer your questi= on, then please post it, along with any comments or suggestions, here in th= is topic, or in a new topic in the EasyLanguage-DLL support forum here: <= a href=3D"https://community.tradestation.com/discussions/forum.aspx?Forum_I= D=3D213&selCategory=3D1853&subCategory=3DEasyLanguage-DLL" target= =3D"_blank">The EasyLanguage-DLL Support Forum.


Kindest r= egards,
Chris Imhof,
EasyLanguage Engineer
TradeStation EasyLa= nguage Consulting
